---

{isLoading && (
  <div class="loading-container">
    <p style={{ textAlign: 'center', padding: '1rem' }}>Loading Surahs...</p>
  </div>
)}

{errorMessage && (
  <div class="error-container">
    <p style={{ color: '#e74c3c', textAlign: 'center', padding: '1rem' }}>
      <strong>⚠️ {errorMessage}</strong><br/>
      <small>Please check your local database or file path.</small>
    </p>
  </div>
)}

{data && data.length > 0 && (
  <div class="numbered-box-container">
    {data.map((item) => (
      <div class="numbered-box" key={item.sura_no}>
        <div class="numbered-box-number">{item.sura_no}</div>
        <div class="numbered-box-content">
          <div class="arabic-name">{item.surah_name_ar}</div>
          <div class="english-name">{item.surah_name_roman}</div>
          <div class="meaning">{item.surah_name_en}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    ))}
  </div>
)}
